Chapter 28

Many false churches will be built up in the last days—They will teach false, vain, and foolish doctrines—Apostasy will abound because of false teachers—The devil will rage in the hearts of men—He will teach all manner of false doctrines. About 559–545 B.C.

1 And now, behold, my brethren, I have spoken unto you, according as the Spirit hath constrained me; wherefore, I know that they must surely come to pass.

2 And the things which shall be written out of the [abook](#note2a) shall be of great [bworth](#note2b) unto the children of men, and especially unto our seed, which is a [cremnant](#note2c) of the house of Israel.

3 For it shall come to pass in that day that the [achurches](#note3a) which are built up, and not unto the Lord, when the one shall say unto the other: Behold, I, I am the Lord’s; and the others shall say: I, I am the Lord’s; and thus shall every one say that hath built up [bchurches](#note3b), and not unto the Lord—

4 And they shall contend one with another; and their priests shall contend one with another, and they shall teach with their [alearning](#note4a), and deny the [bHoly Ghost](#note4b), which giveth utterance.

5 And they [adeny](#note5a) the [bpower](#note5b) of God, the Holy One of Israel; and they say unto the people: Hearken unto us, and hear ye our precept; for behold there is [cno](#note5c) God today, for the Lord and the Redeemer hath done his work, and he hath given his power unto men;

6 Behold, hearken ye unto my precept; if they shall say there is a miracle wrought by the hand of the Lord, believe it not; for this day he is not a God of [amiracles](#note6a); he hath done his work.

7 Yea, and there shall be many which shall say: [aEat](#note7a), drink, and be merry, for tomorrow we die; and it shall be well with us.

8 And there shall also be many which shall say: [aEat](#note8a), drink, and be [bmerry](#note8b); nevertheless, fear God—he will [cjustify](#note8c) in committing a little [dsin](#note8d); yea, [elie](#note8e) a little, take the advantage of one because of his words, dig a [fpit](#note8f) for thy neighbor; there is [gno](#note8g) harm in this; and do all these things, for tomorrow we die; and if it so be that we are guilty, God will beat us with a few stripes, and at last we shall be saved in the kingdom of God.

9 Yea, and there shall be many which shall teach after this manner, [afalse](#note9a) and vain and [bfoolish](#note9b) [cdoctrines](#note9c), and shall be puffed up in their hearts, and shall seek deep to hide their counsels from the Lord; and their works shall be in the dark.

10 And the [ablood](#note10a) of the saints shall cry from the ground against them.

11 Yea, they have all gone out of the [away](#note11a); they have become [bcorrupted](#note11b).

12 Because of [apride](#note12a), and because of [bfalse](#note12b) teachers, and [cfalse doctrine](#note12c), their churches have become corrupted, and their churches are lifted up; because of pride they are puffed up.

13 They [arob](#note13a) the [bpoor](#note13b) because of their fine sanctuaries; they rob the poor because of their fine clothing; and they persecute the meek and the poor in heart, because in their [cpride](#note13c) they are puffed up.

14 They wear [astiff](#note14a) necks and high heads; yea, and because of pride, and wickedness, and abominations, and [bwhoredoms](#note14b), they have all [cgone astray](#note14c) save it be a [dfew](#note14d), who are the humble followers of Christ; nevertheless, they are [eled](#note14e), that in many instances they do [ferr](#note14f) because they are taught by the precepts of men.

15 O the [awise](#note15a), and the learned, and the rich, that are puffed up in the [bpride](#note15b) of their [chearts](#note15c), and all those who preach [dfalse doctrines](#note15d), and all those who commit [ewhoredoms](#note15e), and pervert the right way of the Lord, [fwo](#note15f), wo, wo be unto them, saith the Lord God Almighty, for they shall be thrust down to hell!

16 Wo unto them that [aturn](#note16a) aside the just for a thing of naught and [brevile](#note16b) against that which is good, and say that it is of no worth! For the day shall come that the Lord God will speedily visit the inhabitants of the earth; and in that day that they are [cfully](#note16c) ripe in iniquity they shall perish.

17 But behold, if the inhabitants of the earth shall repent of their wickedness and abominations they shall not be destroyed, saith the Lord of Hosts.

18 But behold, that great and [aabominable](#note18a) church, the [bwhore](#note18b) of all the earth, must [ctumble](#note18c) to the earth, and great must be the fall thereof.

19 For the kingdom of the devil must [ashake](#note19a), and they which belong to it must needs be stirred up unto repentance, or the [bdevil](#note19b) will grasp them with his everlasting [cchains](#note19c), and they be stirred up to anger, and perish;

20 For behold, at that day shall he [arage](#note20a) in the [bhearts](#note20b) of the children of men, and stir them up to anger against that which is good.

21 And others will he [apacify](#note21a), and lull them away into carnal [bsecurity](#note21b), that they will say: All is well in Zion; yea, Zion prospereth, all is well—and thus the [cdevil](#note21c) [dcheateth](#note21d) their souls, and leadeth them away carefully down to hell.

22 And behold, others he [aflattereth](#note22a) away, and telleth them there is no [bhell](#note22b); and he saith unto them: I am no devil, for there is none—and thus he whispereth in their ears, until he grasps them with his awful [cchains](#note22c), from whence there is no deliverance.

23 Yea, they are grasped with death, and hell; and death, and hell, and the devil, and all that have been seized therewith must stand before the throne of God, and be [ajudged](#note23a) according to their works, from whence they must go into the place prepared for them, even a [blake](#note23b) of fire and brimstone, which is endless torment.

24 Therefore, wo be unto him that is at [aease](#note24a) in Zion!

25 Wo be unto him that crieth: All is well!

26 Yea, wo be unto him that [ahearkeneth](#note26a) unto the precepts of men, and denieth the power of God, and the gift of the Holy Ghost!

27 Yea, wo be unto him that saith: We have received, and we [aneed](#note27a) no more!

28 And in fine, wo unto all those who tremble, and are [aangry](#note28a) because of [bthe truth](#note28b) of God! For behold, he that is built upon the [crock](#note28c) [dreceiveth](#note28d) it with gladness; and he that is built upon a sandy foundation trembleth lest he shall fall.

29 Wo be unto him that shall say: We have received the word of God, and we [aneed](#note29a) [bno more](#note29b) of the word of God, for we have enough!

30 For behold, thus saith the Lord God: I will give unto the children of men line upon line, [aprecept](#note30a) upon precept, here a little and there a little; and blessed are those who hearken unto my precepts, and lend an ear unto my counsel, for they shall learn [bwisdom](#note30b); for unto him that [creceiveth](#note30c) I will give [dmore](#note30d); and from them that shall say, We have enough, from them shall be taken away even that which they have.

31 Cursed is he that putteth his [atrust](#note31a) in man, or maketh flesh his arm, or shall hearken unto the [bprecepts](#note31b) of men, save their precepts shall be given by the power of the Holy Ghost.

32 [aWo](#note32a) be unto the Gentiles, saith the Lord God of Hosts! For notwithstanding I shall lengthen out mine arm unto them from day to day, they will deny me; nevertheless, I will be merciful unto them, saith the Lord God, if they will repent and [bcome](#note32b) unto me; for mine [carm](#note32c) is lengthened out all the day long, saith the Lord God of Hosts.

Chapter 29

Many Gentiles will reject the Book of Mormon—They will say, We need no more Bible—The Lord speaks to many nations—He will judge the world out of the books which will be written. About 559–545 B.C.

1 But behold, there shall be many—at that day when I shall proceed to do a [amarvelous work](#note1a) among them, that I may remember my [bcovenants](#note1b) which I have made unto the children of men, that I may set my hand again the [csecond](#note1c) time to recover my people, which are of the house of Israel;

2 And also, that I may remember the promises which I have made unto thee, Nephi, and also unto thy father, that I would remember your seed; and that the [awords](#note2a) of your seed should proceed forth out of my mouth unto your seed; and my words shall [bhiss](#note2b) forth unto the [cends](#note2c) of the earth, for a [dstandard](#note2d) unto my people, which are of the house of Israel;

3 And because my words shall hiss forth—many of the Gentiles shall say: A [aBible](#note3a)! A Bible! We have got a Bible, and there cannot be any more Bible.

4 But thus saith the Lord God: O fools, they shall have a [aBible](#note4a); and it shall proceed forth from the [bJews](#note4b), mine ancient covenant people. And what [cthank](#note4c) they the [dJews](#note4d) for the Bible which they receive from them? Yea, what do the Gentiles mean? Do they remember the travails, and the labors, and the pains of the Jews, and their diligence unto me, in bringing forth salvation unto the Gentiles?

5 O ye Gentiles, have ye remembered the Jews, mine ancient covenant people? Nay; but ye have [acursed](#note5a) them, and have [bhated](#note5b) them, and have not sought to recover them. But behold, I will return all these things upon your own heads; for I the Lord have not forgotten my people.

6 Thou fool, that shall say: A [aBible](#note6a), we have got a Bible, and we need no more Bible. Have ye obtained a Bible save it were by the Jews?

7 Know ye not that there are more [anations](#note7a) than one? Know ye not that I, the Lord your God, have created all men, and that I remember those who are upon the [bisles](#note7b) of the sea; and that I rule in the heavens above and in the [cearth](#note7c) beneath; and I bring forth my [dword](#note7d) unto the children of men, yea, even upon all the nations of the earth?

8 Wherefore murmur ye, because that ye shall receive more of my word? Know ye not that the [atestimony](#note8a) of [btwo](#note8b) nations is a [cwitness](#note8c) unto you that I am God, that I remember one [dnation](#note8d) like unto another? Wherefore, I speak the same words unto one nation like unto another. And when the two [enations](#note8e) shall run together the testimony of the two nations shall run together also.

9 And I do this that I may prove unto many that I am the [asame](#note9a) yesterday, today, and forever; and that I speak forth my [bwords](#note9b) according to mine own pleasure. And because that I have spoken one [cword](#note9c) ye need not suppose that I cannot speak another; for my [dwork](#note9d) is not yet finished; neither shall it be until the end of man, neither from that time henceforth and forever.

10 Wherefore, because that ye have a Bible ye need not suppose that it contains all my [awords](#note10a); neither [bneed](#note10b) ye suppose that I have not caused more to be written.

11 For I command [aall](#note11a) men, both in the east and in the west, and in the north, and in the south, and in the islands of the sea, that they shall [bwrite](#note11b) the words which I speak unto them; for out of the [cbooks](#note11c) which shall be written I will [djudge](#note11d) the world, every man according to their works, according to that which is written.

12 For behold, I shall speak unto the [aJews](#note12a) and they shall [bwrite](#note12b) it; and I shall also speak unto the Nephites and they shall [cwrite](#note12c) it; and I shall also speak unto the other tribes of the house of Israel, which I have led away, and they shall write it; and I shall also speak unto [dall](#note12d) nations of the earth and they shall write it.

13 And it shall come to pass that the [aJews](#note13a) shall have the words of the Nephites, and the Nephites shall have the words of the Jews; and the Nephites and the Jews shall have the words of the [blost tribes](#note13b) of Israel; and the lost tribes of Israel shall have the words of the Nephites and the Jews.

14 And it shall come to pass that my people, which are of the [ahouse of Israel](#note14a), shall be gathered home unto the [blands](#note14b) of their possessions; and my word also shall be gathered in [cone](#note14c). And I will show unto them that fight against my word and against my [dpeople](#note14d), who are of the [ehouse of Israel](#note14e), that I am God, and that I [fcovenanted](#note14f) with [gAbraham](#note14g) that I would remember his [hseed](#note14h) [iforever](#note14i).

Chapter 30

Converted Gentiles will be numbered with the covenant people—Many Lamanites and Jews will believe the word and become delightsome—Israel will be restored and the wicked destroyed. About 559–545 B.C.

1 And now behold, my beloved brethren, I would speak unto you; for I, Nephi, would not suffer that ye should suppose that ye are more righteous than the Gentiles shall be. For behold, except ye shall keep the commandments of God ye shall all likewise [aperish](#note1a); and because of the words which have been spoken ye need not suppose that the Gentiles are utterly destroyed.

2 For behold, I say unto you that as many of the Gentiles as will repent are the [acovenant](#note2a) people of the Lord; and as many of the [bJews](#note2b) as will not repent shall be [ccast off](#note2c); for the Lord [dcovenanteth](#note2d) with none save it be with them that [erepent](#note2e) and believe in his Son, who is the Holy One of Israel.

3 And now, I would prophesy somewhat more concerning the Jews and the Gentiles. For after the book of which I have spoken shall come forth, and be written unto the Gentiles, and sealed up again unto the Lord, there shall be many which shall [abelieve](#note3a) the words which are written; and [bthey](#note3b) shall carry them forth unto the [cremnant](#note3c) of our seed.

4 And then shall the remnant of our seed know concerning us, how that we came out from Jerusalem, and that they are descendants of the Jews.

5 And the gospel of Jesus Christ shall be declared among [athem](#note5a); wherefore, [bthey](#note5b) shall be restored unto the [cknowledge](#note5c) of their fathers, and also to the knowledge of Jesus Christ, which was had among their fathers.

6 And then shall they rejoice; for they shall [aknow](#note6a) that it is a blessing unto them from the hand of God; and their [bscales](#note6b) of darkness shall begin to fall from their eyes; and many generations shall not pass away among them, save they shall be a pure and a [cdelightsome](#note6c) people.

7 And it shall come to pass that the [aJews](#note7a) which are scattered also shall [bbegin](#note7b) to believe in Christ; and they shall begin to gather in upon the face of the land; and as many as shall believe in Christ shall also become a delightsome people.

8 And it shall come to pass that the Lord God shall commence his work among all nations, kindreds, tongues, and people, to bring about the [arestoration](#note8a) of his people upon the earth.

9 And with righteousness shall the [aLord God](#note9a) [bjudge](#note9b) the poor, and reprove with equity for the [cmeek](#note9c) of the earth. And he shall smite the earth with the rod of his mouth; and with the breath of his lips shall he slay the wicked.

10 For the [atime](#note10a) speedily cometh that the Lord God shall cause a great [bdivision](#note10b) among the people, and the wicked will he [cdestroy](#note10c); and he will [dspare](#note10d) his people, yea, even if it so be that he must [edestroy](#note10e) the wicked by fire.

11 And [arighteousness](#note11a) shall be the girdle of his loins, and faithfulness the girdle of his reins.

12 [aAnd](#note12a) then shall the wolf dwell with the lamb; and the leopard shall lie down with the kid, and the calf, and the young lion, and the fatling, together; and a little child shall lead them.

13 And the cow and the bear shall feed; their young ones shall lie down together; and the lion shall eat straw like the ox.

14 And the sucking child shall play on the hole of the asp, and the weaned child shall put his hand on the cockatrice’s den.

15 They shall not hurt nor destroy in all my holy [amountain](#note15a); for the earth shall be full of the [bknowledge](#note15b) of the Lord as the waters cover the sea.

16 Wherefore, the things of [aall](#note16a) nations shall be made known; yea, all things shall be made [bknown](#note16b) unto the children of men.

17 There is nothing which is secret save it shall be [arevealed](#note17a); there is no work of darkness save it shall be made manifest in the light; and there is nothing which is sealed upon the earth save it shall be loosed.

18 Wherefore, all things which have been revealed unto the children of men shall at that [aday](#note18a) be revealed; and Satan shall have power over the hearts of the children of men [bno more](#note18b), for a long time. And now, my beloved brethren, I make an end of my sayings.

Chapter 31

Nephi tells why Christ was baptized—Men must follow Christ, be baptized, receive the Holy Ghost, and endure to the end to be saved—Repentance and baptism are the gate to the strait and narrow path—Eternal life comes to those who keep the commandments after baptism. About 559–545 B.C.

1 And now I, Nephi, make an end of my [aprophesying](#note1a) unto you, my beloved brethren. And I cannot write but a few things, which I know must surely come to pass; neither can I write but a few of the [bwords](#note1b) of my brother Jacob.

2 Wherefore, the things which I have written sufficeth me, save it be a few words which I [amust](#note2a) speak concerning the doctrine of Christ; wherefore, I shall speak unto you plainly, according to the plainness of my prophesying.

3 For my soul delighteth in [aplainness](#note3a); for after this manner doth the Lord God work among the children of men. For the Lord God giveth light unto the [bunderstanding](#note3b); for he speaketh unto men according to their [clanguage](#note3c), unto their understanding.

4 Wherefore, I would that ye should remember that I have spoken unto you concerning that [aprophet](#note4a) which the Lord showed unto me, that should baptize the [bLamb](#note4b) of God, which should take away the sins of the world.

5 And now, if the Lamb of God, he being [aholy](#note5a), should have need to be [bbaptized](#note5b) by water, to fulfil all righteousness, O then, how much more need have we, being unholy, to be [cbaptized](#note5c), yea, even by water!

6 And now, I would ask of you, my beloved brethren, wherein the Lamb of God did fulfil all righteousness in being baptized by water?

7 Know ye not that he was holy? But notwithstanding he being holy, he showeth unto the children of men that, according to the flesh he humbleth himself before the Father, and witnesseth unto the Father that he would be [aobedient](#note7a) unto him in keeping his commandments.

8 Wherefore, after he was baptized with water the Holy Ghost descended upon him in the [aform](#note8a) of a [bdove](#note8b).

9 And again, it showeth unto the children of men the straitness of the path, and the narrowness of the [agate](#note9a), by which they should enter, he having set the [bexample](#note9b) before them.

10 And he said unto the children of men: [aFollow](#note10a) thou me. Wherefore, my beloved brethren, can we [bfollow](#note10b) Jesus save we shall be willing to keep the commandments of the Father?

11 And the Father said: Repent ye, repent ye, and be baptized in the name of my Beloved Son.

12 And also, the voice of the Son came unto me, saying: He that is baptized in my name, to him will the Father [agive](#note12a) the Holy Ghost, like unto me; wherefore, [bfollow](#note12b) me, and do the things which ye have seen me do.

13 Wherefore, my beloved brethren, I know that if ye shall [afollow](#note13a) the Son, with full purpose of heart, acting no [bhypocrisy](#note13b) and no deception before God, but with real [cintent](#note13c), repenting of your sins, witnessing unto the Father that ye are [dwilling](#note13d) to take upon you the [ename](#note13e) of Christ, by [fbaptism](#note13f)—yea, by following your Lord and your Savior down into the water, according to his word, behold, then shall ye receive the Holy Ghost; yea, then cometh the [gbaptism of fire](#note13g) and of the Holy Ghost; and then can ye speak with the [htongue](#note13h) of angels, and shout praises unto the Holy One of Israel.

14 But, behold, my beloved brethren, thus came the voice of the Son unto me, saying: After ye have repented of your sins, and witnessed unto the Father that ye are willing to keep my commandments, by the baptism of water, and have received the baptism of fire and of the Holy Ghost, and can speak with a new tongue, yea, even with the tongue of angels, and after this should [adeny](#note14a) me, it would have been [bbetter](#note14b) for you that ye had not known me.

15 And I heard a voice from the Father, saying: Yea, the [awords](#note15a) of my Beloved are true and faithful. He that [bendureth](#note15b) to the [cend](#note15c), the same shall be saved.

16 And now, my beloved brethren, I know by this that unless a man shall [aendure](#note16a) to the end, in following the [bexample](#note16b) of the Son of the living God, he cannot be saved.

17 Wherefore, do the things which I have told you I have seen that your Lord and your Redeemer should do; for, for this cause have they been shown unto me, that ye might know the gate by which ye should enter. For the gate by which ye should enter is repentance and [abaptism](#note17a) by water; and then cometh a [bremission](#note17b) of your sins by fire and by the Holy Ghost.

18 And then are ye in this [astrait](#note18a) and narrow [bpath](#note18b) which leads to eternal life; yea, ye have entered in by the gate; ye have done according to the commandments of the Father and the Son; and ye have received the Holy Ghost, which [cwitnesses](#note18c) of the [dFather](#note18d) and the Son, unto the fulfilling of the promise which he hath made, that if ye entered in by the way ye should receive.

19 And now, my beloved brethren, after ye have gotten into this strait and narrow [apath](#note19a), I would ask if all is [bdone](#note19b)? Behold, I say unto you, Nay; for ye have not come thus far save it were by the word of Christ with unshaken [cfaith](#note19c) in him, [drelying](#note19d) wholly upon the merits of him who is mighty to [esave](#note19e).

20 Wherefore, ye must press forward with a [asteadfastness](#note20a) in Christ, having a perfect brightness of [bhope](#note20b), and a [clove](#note20c) of God and of all men. Wherefore, if ye shall press forward, feasting upon the word of Christ, and [dendure](#note20d) to the end, behold, thus saith the Father: Ye shall have [eeternal life](#note20e).

21 And now, behold, my beloved brethren, this is the [away](#note21a); and there is [bnone](#note21b) other way nor [cname](#note21c) given under heaven whereby man can be saved in the kingdom of God. And now, behold, this is the [ddoctrine](#note21d) of Christ, and the only and true doctrine of the [eFather](#note21e), and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost, which is [fone God](#note21f), without end. Amen.

Chapter 32

Angels speak by the power of the Holy Ghost—Men must pray and gain knowledge for themselves from the Holy Ghost. About 559–545 B.C.

1 And now, behold, my beloved brethren, I suppose that ye ponder somewhat in your hearts concerning that which ye should do after ye have entered in by the way. But, behold, why do ye ponder these things in your hearts?

2 Do ye not remember that I said unto you that after ye had [areceived](#note2a) the Holy Ghost ye could speak with the [btongue](#note2b) of angels? And now, how could ye speak with the tongue of angels save it were by the Holy Ghost?

3 [aAngels](#note3a) speak by the power of the Holy Ghost; wherefore, they speak the words of Christ. Wherefore, I said unto you, [bfeast](#note3b) upon the [cwords](#note3c) of Christ; for behold, the words of Christ will [dtell](#note3d) you all things what ye should do.

4 Wherefore, now after I have spoken these words, if ye cannot understand them it will be because ye [aask](#note4a) not, neither do ye knock; wherefore, ye are not brought into the light, but must perish in the dark.

5 For behold, again I say unto you that if ye will enter in by the way, and receive the Holy Ghost, it will [ashow](#note5a) unto you all things what ye should do.

6 Behold, this is the doctrine of Christ, and there will be no more doctrine given until after he shall [amanifest](#note6a) himself unto you in the flesh. And when he shall manifest himself unto you in the flesh, the things which he shall say unto you shall ye observe to do.

7 And now I, Nephi, cannot say more; the Spirit stoppeth mine utterance, and I am left to mourn because of the [aunbelief](#note7a), and the wickedness, and the ignorance, and the [bstiffneckedness](#note7b) of men; for they will [cnot](#note7c) search [dknowledge](#note7d), nor understand great knowledge, when it is given unto them in [eplainness](#note7e), even as plain as word can be.

8 And now, my beloved brethren, I perceive that ye ponder still in your hearts; and it grieveth me that I must speak concerning this thing. For if ye would hearken unto the [aSpirit](#note8a) which teacheth a man to [bpray](#note8b), ye would know that ye must [cpray](#note8c); for the [devil spirit](#note8d) teacheth not a man to pray, but teacheth him that he must not pray.

9 But behold, I say unto you that ye must [apray](#note9a) always, and not faint; that ye must not perform any thing unto the Lord save in the first place ye shall [bpray](#note9b) unto the Father in the [cname](#note9c) of Christ, that he will [dconsecrate](#note9d) thy performance unto thee, that thy performance may be for the [ewelfare](#note9e) of thy soul.

Chapter 33

Nephi’s words are true—They testify of Christ—Those who believe in Christ will believe Nephi’s words, which will stand as a witness before the judgment bar. About 559–545 B.C.

1 And now I, Nephi, cannot write all the things which were taught among my people; neither am I [amighty](#note1a) in writing, like unto speaking; for when a man [bspeaketh](#note1b) by the power of the Holy Ghost the power of the Holy Ghost carrieth it unto the hearts of the children of men.

2 But behold, there are many that [aharden](#note2a) their [bhearts](#note2b) against the [cHoly Spirit](#note2c), that it hath no place in them; wherefore, they cast many things away which are written and esteem them as things of naught.

3 But I, Nephi, have written what I have written, and I esteem it as of great [aworth](#note3a), and especially unto my people. For I [bpray](#note3b) continually for them by day, and mine [ceyes](#note3c) water my pillow by night, because of them; and I cry unto my God in faith, and I know that he will hear my cry.

4 And I know that the Lord God will consecrate my prayers for the gain of my people. And the words which I have written in weakness will be made strong unto them; for it [apersuadeth](#note4a) them to do good; it maketh known unto them of their fathers; and it speaketh of Jesus, and persuadeth them to believe in him, and to endure to the end, which is life [beternal](#note4b).

5 And it speaketh [aharshly](#note5a) against sin, according to the [bplainness](#note5b) of the truth; wherefore, no man will be angry at the words which I have written save he shall be of the spirit of the devil.

6 I [aglory](#note6a) in [bplainness](#note6b); I glory in truth; I glory in my Jesus, for he hath [credeemed](#note6c) my soul from hell.

7 I have [acharity](#note7a) for my people, and great faith in Christ that I shall meet many souls spotless at his judgment-seat.

8 I have charity for the [aJew](#note8a)—I say Jew, because I mean them from whence I came.

9 I also have charity for the Gentiles. But behold, for none of [athese](#note9a) can I hope except they shall be [breconciled](#note9b) unto Christ, and enter into the [cnarrow](#note9c) [dgate](#note9d), and [ewalk](#note9e) in the [fstrait](#note9f) path which leads to life, and continue in the path until the end of the day of [gprobation](#note9g).

10 And now, my beloved brethren, and also [aJew](#note10a), and all ye ends of the earth, hearken unto these words and [bbelieve](#note10b) in Christ; and if ye believe not in these words believe in Christ. And if ye shall [cbelieve](#note10c) in Christ ye will believe in these [dwords](#note10d), for they are the [ewords](#note10e) of Christ, and he hath given them unto me; and they [fteach](#note10f) all men that they should do good.

11 And if they are not the words of Christ, judge ye—for Christ will show unto you, with [apower](#note11a) and great [bglory](#note11b), that they are his words, at the last day; and you and I shall stand face to face before his bar; and ye shall know that I have been commanded of him to write these things, notwithstanding my weakness.

12 And I pray the Father in the name of Christ that many of us, if not all, may be saved in his [akingdom](#note12a) at that great and last day.

13 And now, my beloved brethren, all those who are of the house of Israel, and all ye ends of the earth, I speak unto you as the voice of one [acrying](#note13a) from the dust: Farewell until that great day shall come.

14 And you that will not partake of the goodness of God, and respect the words of the [aJews](#note14a), and also my [bwords](#note14b), and the words which shall proceed forth out of the mouth of the Lamb of God, behold, I bid you an everlasting farewell, for these words shall [ccondemn](#note14c) you at the last day.

15 For what I seal on earth, shall be brought against you at the [ajudgment](#note15a) bar; for thus hath the Lord commanded me, and I must [bobey](#note15b). Amen.
